### Simultaneous Substitution

### Reflexive and transitive closure

### Lookup 

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="9544" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Problem3._∋_⦂_"></a><a id="9549" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9549" class="Datatype Operator">_∋_⦂_</a> <a id="9555" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9557" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#8865" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="9565" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9567" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#8796" class="Function">Id</a> <a id="9570" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9572" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#8686" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="9577" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9579" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="9583" class="Keyword">where</a>

    <a id="Problem3._∋_⦂_.Z"></a><a id="9594" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9594" class="InductiveConstructor">Z</a> <a id="9596" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9598" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="9600" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9601" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9601" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9603" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9603" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9605" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9605" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9606" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="9616" class="Comment">--------------------</a>
      <a id="9643" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9645" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9601" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9647" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#8909" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9649" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9603" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9651" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#8909" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⦂</a> <a id="9653" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9605" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9655" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9549" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="9657" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9603" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9659" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9549" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="9661" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9605" class="Bound">A</a>
